ftext "lua"
# Searches for text in all files in the current folder
function ftext
if test (count $argv) -lt 1
echo "Usage: ftext <pattern>"
return 1
end

set -l output (grep -iIHrn --color=always -- "$argv[1]" . ^/dev/null)

if test -z "$output"
echo "No matches found."
return 1
end

set -l lines (string split \n -- "$output" | count)
set -l screen_lines (tput lines)

if test "$lines" -gt "$screen_lines"
printf '%s\n' "$output" | less -R
else
printf '%s\n' "$output"
end
end

function clia
read -l line; commandline -a $line
# commandline -a 
end

bind -M insert \et 'fuzzy_complete'

function fuzzy_complete
complete -C | sort -u | fzf --height 40% --multi --reverse -q (commandline -t) | cut --output-delimiter ' ' -f1 | sed 's/-//g' | clia
commandline -f end-of-line 
end

load_shell_globals
function load_shell_globals
set -l files "$HOME/.config/shell/envvars" "$HOME/.config/shell/aliases"
set -l sources ""

for file in $files
if test -f $file
set sources "$sources; source $file"
end
end

test -n "$sources"; and replay (string trim --chars='; ' -- $sources)
end

awk '{
  w = length($0);
  for (i = 1; i <= w; i++) {
    x = i - w / 2;
    y = NR - NR_TOTAL / 2;
    r = sqrt(x * x + y * y);
    if (r < RADIUS) {
      printf "%s", substr($0, i, 1);
    } else {
      printf " ";
    }
  }
  print "";
}' NR_TOTAL=$(wc -l < ascii.txt) RADIUS=30 ascii.txt

function fzfedit
set -l file (tree -Fifa --noreport | tail -n +2 | sed 's|^\./||' | fzf --height 40% --layout=reverse --border)
test -n "$file" && echo "$file" | xargs -r nvim
end

trash-restore-direct ./
function trash-restore-direct
    set file_path $argv[1]
    set trash_index (trash-list | grep -F $file_path | awk '{print $1}')
    trash-restore $trash_index
end
